### [1] [Roots Beneath the Cut: Uncovering the Risk of Concept Revival in Pruning-Based Unlearning for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06640)
*Ci Zhang,Zhaojun Ding,Chence Yang,Jun Liu,Xiaoming Zhai,Shaoyi Huang,Beiwen Li,Xiaolong Ma,Jin Lu,Geng Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

Innovation Snapshot: 揭示了剪枝遗忘方法的安全漏洞，提出无需数据和训练即可从剪枝扩散模型中恢复被擦除概念的攻击框架。

### [3] [Margin-Consistent Deep Subtyping of Invasive Lung Adenocarcinoma via Perturbation Fidelity in Whole-Slide Image Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06650)

### [5] [A Parameter-efficient Convolutional Approach for Weed Detection in Multispectral Aerial Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06655)
*Leo Thomas Ramos,Angel D. Sappa*

Main category: cs.CV

Innovation Snapshot: FCBNet introduces a frozen ConvNeXt backbone with Feature Correction Blocks for efficient weed segmentation, achieving >85% mIoU with 90% fewer trainable parameters.


### [6] [GameVerse: Can Vision-Language Models Learn from Video-based Reflection?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06656)

### [7] [EnsAug: Augmentation-Driven Ensembles for Human Motion Sequence Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06661)

Main category: cs.CV

Innovation Snapshot: HyperTokens introduces a transformer-based token generator for continual VideoQA that produces task-specific tokens on demand with meta-inspired regularisation to suppress forgetting and enable cross-modal transfer.
